---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: kanna
---

###  kanna₁

* _a noun refering to any plant of the genus Canna having large sheathing leaves and clusters of large showy flowers (FinnWordNet) but overlaps forms of *kantaa* (to carry)._
* UPOS:  NOUN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  9
* Origins:
